<a class="elementor-accordion-title" tabindex="0">SENIOR CENTRE LEADER</a>

<div id="elementor-tab-content-4171" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix elementor-active" data-tab="1" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-4171" style="display: none;"><p>The Senior Centre Leader has a span of influence over a cluster of centres and their respective Centre Leaders. He/she plays an active role as Mentor to Centre Leaders, guiding them in the development of strategic plans and structures, ensuring Centre operations adhere to ECDA regulations and strict compliance with E-Bridge’s Standard Operating Procedures (SOPs).</p><p>Steeped in pedagogical knowledge and leadership, the Senior Centre Leader upholds curriculum and organisational excellence by mentoring Centre Leaders in effective leadership, quality of curriculum and operational efficiency.</p><p><strong>Job Requirements:</strong></p><ul><li>A recognised Bachelor degree in Early Childhood Education from an approved institution with a Diploma in Early Childhood Care &amp; Education (Leadership) or its equivalent</li><li>At least 10 years relevant working experience in the EC sector with at least 5 years in a leadership role managing a 200-500 children capacity cluster</li><li>Possess High EQ, matured and exemplary leadership</li><li>Exceptional interpersonal &amp; management skills</li><li>Excellent written and verbal communicational skills in English and Mandarin</li><li>Knowledge of or willingness to acquire knowledge of inquiry based learning is required</li><li>Passionate and dedicated in growing and developing the next generation of Centre Leaders</li><li>Multi-lingual in English, Mandarin, Malay or Tamil will be favourably considered</li></ul><p>If you meet the above criteria and are excited to begin a rewarding career with a people centric pre-school, we welcome you to apply in confidence by submitting your resume to <a href="mailto:careers@e-bridge.edu.sg"><strong>careers@e-bridge.edu.sg</strong></a></p></div>
</div>

He/she leads by fostering a shared vision among staff and upholds quality by nurturing professionalism and a culture of care, respect and collaboration within the Centre.</p><p>The Centre Leader also inspires professionalism through role modelling, and guiding the staff in designing and implementing a holistic curriculum underlined by E-Bridge’s values and philosophy.</p><p><strong>Job Requirements:</strong></p><ul><li>A recognised Bachelor degree in Early Childhood Education from an approved institution and Diploma in Early Childhood Care &amp; Education (Leadership) or its equivalent</li><li>Knowledge of or willingness to acquire knowledge of inquiry based learning is required</li><li>Strong management skills preferred (e.g. attention to details, problem solving and knowledge of quality standards and instruments.)</li><li>Excellent written and verbal communication skills</li><li>Passionate and dedication leaders whom are great motivators and developer of people</li><li>Multi-lingual in English, Mandarin, Malay or Tamil will be considered favorably</li></ul><p>If you meet the above criteria and are excited to begin a rewarding career with a people centric pre-school, we welcome you to apply in confidence by submitting your resume to&nbsp;<a href="mailto:careers@e-bridge.edu.sg"><strong>careers@e-bridge.edu.sg</strong></a></p></div>

The Deputy Centre Leader also mentors the Senior Preschool Teachers within the centre and oversees the development of professional competence of the teachers.</p><p>In the absence of the Centre Leaders, the Deputy Centre Leader steps up to oversee the management of Centre operations.</p><p><strong>Job Requirements:</strong></p><ul><li>Bachelor in Early Childhood Care &amp; Education (Teaching) and/or Advanced Diploma in Early Childhood Leadership (ADECL)</li><li>At least 5 years teaching experience in a pre-school environment</li><li>Knowledge of inquiry based learning is required</li><li>Exceptional interpersonal skills</li><li>Excellent written and verbal communication skills</li><li>We seek only passionate and dedicated educators whom can make a difference in children’s learning</li></ul><p>If you meet the above criteria and are excited to begin a rewarding career with a people centric pre-school, we welcome you to apply in confidence by submitting your resume to&nbsp;<a href="mailto:careers@e-bridge.edu.sg"><strong>careers@e-bridge.edu.sg</strong></a></p></div>

<div id="elementor-tab-content-4174" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="4" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-4174" style="display: none;"><p>The Senior Preschool Teacher mentors teachers to enhance their teaching practice including the nurturing of trusting and respectful relationships with children. He/she utilises in-depth subject knowledge and pedagogical expertise to design and implement a developmentally and culturally appropriate curriculum for children, and contributes to innovations in teaching and learning practices.</p><p>As an experienced early childhood educator, the Senior Preschool Teacher oversees the design and set up of secure and quality learning environments for children. He/she develops structures for sustained collaborative partnerships with families and communities, and supports the pedagogy team in fostering a culture of continuous learning, collaboration and collegiality within the centre.</p><p><strong>Job Requirements:</strong></p><ul><li>Diploma in Early Childhood Care &amp; Education (Teaching) with 5 GCE ‘O’ Levels with English at Grade B4 or its equivalent</li><li>At least 5 years teaching experience in a similar setting</li><li>Knowledge of or willingness to acquire knowledge of inquiry based learning is required</li><li>Exceptional interpersonal skills with sound working knowledge of Ms Office</li><li>Excellent written and verbal communication skills</li><li>Multi-lingual in English, Mandarin, Malay or Tamil</li><li>We seek only passionate and dedicated educators whom can make a difference in children’s learning</li></ul><p>If you meet the above criteria and are excited to begin a rewarding career with a people centric pre-school, we welcome you to apply in confidence by submitting your resume to&nbsp;<a href="mailto:careers@e-bridge.edu.sg"><strong>careers@e-bridge.edu.sg</strong></a></p></div>

<a class="elementor-accordion-title" tabindex="0">PRESCHOOL TEACHER (ENGLISH)</a>

<div id="elementor-tab-content-4175" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="5" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-4175" style="display: none;"><p>The Preschool Teacher effectively creates a secure and quality learning environment for children, through enhancing trusting and respectful relationships with them. He/she enriches children’s learning through codesigning and implementing a developmentally and culturally appropriate curriculum, while effectively integrating innovative teaching and learning practices.</p><p>The Preschool Teacher is also proactive and intentional in strengthening partnerships with families and the community, and codesigns collaborative efforts with colleagues and stakeholders to achieve this goal. As an experienced early childhood educator, the Preschool Teacher guides teachers in enhancing their practice and engages in continuous learning and reflective practice.</p><p><strong>Job Requirements:</strong></p><ul><li>Diploma in Early Childhood Care &amp; Education (Teaching) or its equivalent with 5 GCE ‘O’ Levels with English at Grade B4</li><li>At least 2 years teaching experience in a similar setting</li><li>Knowledge of or willingness to acquire knowledge of inquiry based learning is required</li><li>Excellent written and verbal communication skills&nbsp;</li><li>We seek only passionate and dedicated educators whom can make a difference in children’s learning</li></ul><p>If you meet the above criteria and are excited to begin a rewarding career with a people centric pre-school, we welcome you to apply in confidence by submitting your resume to&nbsp;<a href="mailto:careers@e-bridge.edu.sg"><strong>careers@e-bridge.edu.sg</strong></a></p></div>

<div id="elementor-tab-content-4178" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="8" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-4178" style="display: none;"><p>Learning Support teachers are to ensure children with mild learning difficulties achieve maximum proficiency in literacy and numeracy before leaving the pre-school setting for either mainstream primary school or a SPEd school. Learning support educators focus on the provision of supplementary teaching to children who require additional help. They work with children in groups or one-to-one, either in the classroom or through the scheduled Learning support packages (Literacy, Language, Fine Motor &amp; Social Skill Group) for the children identified, in-class support for children in the DS Programme and plan for progressive strategies for children enrolled in EIPIC.</p><p>The Learning Support Educator also follow thru with identifying the developmental needs of the child during screening by conducting both standardised (e.g. for general development and literacy) and non-standardised assessments (e.g. observations and child’s work samples). He/she creates a secure environment for young children through nurturing respectful, responsive and reciprocal relationships with them.</p><p>The Teaching Assistant/Para-educarer is intentional in building trusting and respectful partnerships with parents and families. He/she actively engages in centre initiatives and supports its collaborative efforts with the community. He/she also works closely with colleagues and contributes to a culture of collaboration and collegiality.</p><p>As an early childhood educator, the Teaching Assistant/Para-educarer engages in continuous learning and reflective practice.</p><p>Fresh graduates from Fundamentals Certificate in Early Childhood Care and Education (FECCE) or students who are currently undergoing Early Childhood relevant courses are welcome to apply.</p><p><strong><u>Job Requirements</u></strong></p><ul><li>Obtained a Fundamentals Certificate in Early Childhood Care and Education (FECCE) or its equivalent</li><li>At least Secondary 2 education or 8 years of formal education and attained an average level of 4 under the Statement of Attainment (SOA) in Employability Skills (ES) WSQ Workplace Literacy (WPL) series</li><li>Exceptional interpersonal skills</li><li>Excellent written and verbal communication skills</li><li>Show passion, dedication and willingness to make a difference in children’s learning</li></ul><p>If you meet the above criteria and are excited to begin a rewarding career with a people centric pre-school, we welcome you to apply in confidence by submitting your resume to&nbsp;<a href="mailto:careers@e-bridge.edu.sg"><strong>careers@e-bridge.edu.sg</strong></a></p></div>

The right candidate will be offered opportunities for sponsorship of higher ECCE courses.</p><p><strong>Job Requirements</strong></p><ul><li>At least Secondary 2 education or 8 years of formal education and attained an average level of 4 under the Statement of Attainment (SOA) in Employability Skills (ES) WSQ Workplace Literacy (WPL) series</li><li>Excellent written and verbal communication skills</li><li>Exceptional interpersonal skills with sound working knowledge of MS Office</li><li>Passionate to work with children and make a difference to children’s learning</li><li>Mid-career entrants are welcome to apply.</li></ul><p>If you meet the above criteria and is excited to begin a rewarding career with a people centric pre-school, we welcome you to apply in confidence via <a href="https://e-bridgecareers.peoplestrong.com">Apply Now</a>&nbsp; or drop your CV to <a href="mailto:careers@e-bridge.edu.sg"><strong>careers@e-bridge.edu.sg</strong></a></p></div>

<script type="text/javascript">
				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const dataAttribute = 'data-e-bg-lazyload';
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `[${ dataAttribute }]:not(.lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
					entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
						if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
							let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
							const lazyloadSelector = lazyloadBackground.getAttribute( dataAttribute );
							if ( lazyloadSelector ) {
								lazyloadBackground = entry.target.querySelector( lazyloadSelector );
							}
							if( lazyloadBackground ) {
								lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'lazyloaded' );
							}
							lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
						}
					});
					}, { rootMargin: '100px 0px 100px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>
